He’s a physically gifted athlete, but his plate discipline is among the worst in the league. He has a hyper-aggressive approach, but it didn’t help him to avoid strikeouts. Even with some serious flaws, he had a successful 343 plate appearance debut, batting .288/.338/.473 with 12 home runs. That’s 10% better than league average (110 wRC ). A combination of hard, low angle contact led to a high batting average on balls in play. While his .375 BABIP will probably serve as a career high, he should consistently outperform league average. Of greater concern is his 19% swinging strike rate. Only a few players had similar contact issues – namely Danny Espinosa, Joey Gallo, Javier Baez, Miguel Sano, and Chris Carter. The 24-year-old won’t be handed an opportunity in 2018. He’ll have to compete with Aaron Altherr and Roman Quinn for playing time. (Brad Johnson)",
